[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'u'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:** When `state.ptr` points to [0m[32m'n'[0m[39m, we need to read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters total [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mn, u, l, l[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The check must verify at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes are available.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix the [0m[32m'true'[0m[39m keyword parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m602[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `src/json.[0m[1;92mc:602[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current code:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'r'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:** When `state.ptr` points to [0m[32m't'[0m[39m, we need to read [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m characters total [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mt, r, u, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The check must verify at least [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes are available.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Fix the [0m[32m'false'[0m[39m keyword parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m618[0m[1;39m)[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location:** `src/json.[0m[1;92mc:618[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Current code:**[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Fixed code:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mend - state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m || *[0m[1;39m([0m[39m++ state.ptr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m != [0m[32m'a'[0m[39m ||[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale:** When `state.ptr` points to [0m[32m'f'[0m[39m, we need to read [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m characters total [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mf, a, l, s, e[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The check must verify at least [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m bytes are available.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Directly addresses the root cause:** The fix corrects the off-by-one error in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary calculations that causes the heap-buffer-overflow.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows existing correct patterns:** The fix aligns with the boundary checking[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern already used successfully in Unicode escape parsing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m323[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Minimal and surgical changes:** Only three integer constants are changed, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreducing the risk of introducing new bugs.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Comprehensive coverage:** Unlike the previous patch that only fixed [0m[32m'true'[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis fixes all three vulnerable keyword parsers.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves all existing logic:** The fix only corrects the boundary checks; all[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother parsing logic, error handling, two-pass architecture, and memory management [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremain unchanged.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Codebase Logic[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Two-pass parsing preserved:** The fix works correctly in both first and second[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpass, as it only affects boundary validation.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Error handling unchanged:** When the boundary check fails [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcorrectly now[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode still jumps to `e_unknown_value` as intended.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No impact on valid inputs:** For well-formed JSON with complete keywords, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchecks will pass as before [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., for [0m[32m"null"[0m[39m: `[0m[1;36m4[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` is false, so parsing [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinues[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Consistent with parser design:** The `end` pointer semantics [0m[1;39m([0m[39mone byte past [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalid buffer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are maintained.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Fixes the crash location:** Line [0m[1;36m634[0m[39m in [0m[32m'null'[0m[39m parsing is corrected by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchanging line [0m[1;36m633[0m[39m's check from `< [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m` to `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m`.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Prevents the [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte overflow:** With the correct check, the parser will detect[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsufficient buffer space before attempting to read beyond bounds.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Handles the fuzzer test case:** Truncated inputs like [0m[32m"nul"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m3[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will now[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbe caught by the boundary check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m < [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` is true[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, triggering `e_unknown_value` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstead of overflowing.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Addresses CWE-[0m[1;36m126[0m[39m:** The fix prevents the buffer over-read by ensuring [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary checks account for all bytes to be read.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Slightly more restrictive parsing**[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Description:** The parser will now reject JSON inputs that end exactly with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mincomplete keywords [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[32m"nul"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"tru"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"fals"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** This is the intended behavior. Incomplete keywords are invalid [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJSON and should be rejected. The error message [0m[32m"Unknown value"[0m[39m correctly describes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe issue.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: No performance impact**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Description:** The fix changes integer comparison constants, which has [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnegligible performance impact.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m needed.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: No ABI/API changes**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Description:** The function signatures and return values are unchanged.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Mitigation:** [0m[3;35mNone[0m[39m needed; existing code using the parser will work without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe correct boundary checking pattern is already implemented in the same file:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Lines [0m[1;36m306[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m310[0m[39m:** Unicode escape sequence parsing correctly checks `< [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` before [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreading [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Lines [0m[1;36m323[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m327[0m[39m:** Surrogate pair parsing correctly checks `< [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m` before reading [0m[1;36m6[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese demonstrate that the codebase already uses this pattern successfully, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirming the fix strategy's correctness.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Implementation Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
